For the past 20 years, Fitch Ratings‚Äô Emerging Market Sovereign Credit Index (EM SCI), an unweighted average of EM sovereign ratings, has been closely correlated with the US dollar: a stronger dollar was associated with lower EM sovereign ratings, and vice-versa. In this context, the recent depreciation of the dollar should be supportive of EM sovereign ratings, all else equal.
